nāma nāmena Kassapo iti maṃ vidū  suddhimaggaṃ gavesanto vasāmi Kosiketadā   ApTha Padumuttaro nāma jino sabbadhammāna pāragū  vivekakāmo sambuddho āgacchi anilañjasā ApTha Vanagge gacchamānassa disvā raṃsiṃ mahesino  kaṭṭhamañcaṃ paññapetvāna ajinañ ca apatthariṃ ApTha Āsanaṃ paññapetvāna sire katvāna añjaliṃ  somanassaṃ pavedetvāimaṃ vacanam abraviṃ   ApTha Sallakatto tuvaṃ vīra āturānaṃ tikicchako  mamaṃrogaparetassatikicchaṃ dehi nāyaka ApTha Kallaṭṭhikā yepassanti Buddhaseṭṭha tavammune  dhuvaṃ ti siddhiṃpapponti etesaṃ jajjaro bhavo ApTha Na me deyyaṃ tavamatthi pavattaphalabhoji haṃ  idaṃ me āsanam atthi nisīda kaṭṭhamañcake   ApTha Nisīdi tattha bhagavā asambhītova kesarī  muhuttaṃ vītināmetvā imaṃ vacanam abravi   ApTha ‘Vissaṭṭho hohi mā bhāyi laddho jotiraso tayā  yaṃ tuyhaṃ patthitaṃ sabbaṃ paripūressati nāgate ApTha Na thokaṃ taṃ kataṃ tuyhaṃ puññakkhette anuttare  sakkā uddharitum attā yassa cittaṃ paṇīhitaṃ ApTha Iminā āsanadānena cetanāpanidhīhi ca sampatte evaṃ cintes ahaṃ tadā   ApTha Nacchannaṃ nappaṭirūpaṃ jānantassa guṇāguṇaṃ  yo haṃ saṅghe adatvāna aggaṃ bhuñjeyya maṃ tadā   ApTha Ayaṃ Buddho asamasamo battiṃsavaralakkhaṇo  tato pabhāvitosaṅgho puññakkhetto anuttaro   ApTha Tattha dassāmahaṃ dānaṃ navasassaṃ pure pure  evāhaṃ cintayitvāna haṭṭho pīṇitamānaso ApTha Khettato dhaññam āharitvā sambuddham upasaṅkamiṃ  upasaṅkamma sambuddhaṃ lokajeṭṭhaṃ narāsabhaṃ  vanditvā satthuno pāde imaṃ vacanam abraviṃ   ApTha Navasassañ ca sampannamāyāgopi ca taṃmune  anukampam upādāya adhivāsehi cakkhumā   ApTha Padumuttaro lokavidū āhutīnaṃ paṭiggaho  mamaṃ saṅkappam aññāya imaṃ vacanam abraviṃ   ApTha Cattāro ca paṭipannā cattāro ca phale ṭhitā  esa saṅgho ujubhūto paññāsīlasamāhito   ApTha Yajantānaṃ manussānaṃ puññapekkhāna pāṇinaṃ  karontaṃ opadhikaṃpuññaṃ saṅghe dinnaṃ mahapphalaṃ   ApTha Tasmiṃ saṅghe ca dātabbaṃ navasassaṃ tathetaraṃ  saṅghato uddisitvāna bhikkhūnetvāna saṃgharaṃ  paṭiyattaṃ ghare yan tebhikkhusaṅghassa dehi tvaṃ   ApTha Saṅghato uddisitvāna bhikkhūnetvāna haṃ gharaṃ  yaṃ ghare paṭiyattaṃ me bhikkhusaṅghassa dās ahaṃ   ApTha Tena kammena sukatena cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca  jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ Tāvatiṃsam agacch ahaṃ   ApTha Tattha me sukataṃ vyamhaṃsovaṇṇaṃ sappabhassaraṃ  saṭṭhiyojanam ubbiddhaṃ tiṃsayojanavitthataṃ   ApTha Ākiṇṇaṃ bhavanaṃ mayhaṃ nārīgaṇasamākulaṃ  tatthabhutvā pivitvā ca vasāmi Tidase ahaṃ   ApTha Satānaṃ tīṇikkhattuñ ca devarajjam akārayiṃ  satānaṃ pañcakkhattuñ ca cakkavattī ahos ahaṃ  padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ   ApTha  S phalinaṃ S
